- **Phase 5 slice 5BC.2b (flow-sensitive branch merging + E0371) landed:** [cplus-core/src/borrowck.rs](cplus-core/src/borrowck.rs). The analyzer is now flow-sensitive across `if`/`else`, `match` arms, and loop bodies:
  - **`merge_branches` free function** computes the post-join state by intersecting per-place states across the live (non-diverging) arms via `PlaceState::merge`. The `MaybePartial` state appears for the first time when one branch moves a binding and another doesn't — Owned ∩ Moved = MaybePartial.
  - **`walk_block_in_scope`** retains only bindings present in the outer scope after walking a block; branch-local `let`s no longer leak past their closing brace.
  - **`walk_loop_body`** runs the body once from a snapshot, then merges the post-body state with the pre-loop state — modeling "body might not run." Any move inside the body becomes `MaybePartial` post-loop. Conservative (matches Rust's rule; tightening requires a real iteration-count analysis we don't have).
  - **Divergence detection** reuses `lower::block_diverges` / `expr_diverges` / `stmt_diverges` (already `pub(crate)` from slice 4-end). A branch ending in `return`/`break`/`continue` is excluded from the merge — its post-state is unreachable from the join. If every arm diverges, the join itself is unreachable and the state carries forward pre-branch (the code below the join is dead).
  - **E0371 — use of possibly-moved binding**. Fires when a bare `ExprKind::Ident` read encounters a place in `MaybePartial` state and the binding is provably non-Copy (same `CopyOracle` gate as E0370). The move-arg path in `apply_call` also routes through `record_read`, so trying to *move* a possibly-moved binding fires too. Each E0371 carries a `MaybeIncorrect` suggestion to clone before the branch.
  - **Honest caveat recorded in the module docs:** sema's linear E0335 today fires on `if c { move x; } use(x);` patterns (sema isn't flow-sensitive), and the pipeline bails before borrowck runs. So **E0371 rarely fires in user-visible cases yet** — the machinery is infrastructure for a later slice that will replace sema's overly-conservative E0335 with borrowck's flow-sensitive version. State-dump unit tests demonstrate the merging works correctly today; the production diagnostic surfaces value once the sema integration lands.
  - **Tests**: 7 new unit tests + 1 updated. New: `asymmetric_if_move_produces_maybe_partial` (pinning Owned ∩ Moved = MaybePartial), `symmetric_if_move_in_both_branches_is_moved` (Moved ∩ Moved = Moved, not MaybePartial), `diverging_branch_excluded_from_merge` (return in the move-branch leaves the join with Owned), `branch_local_let_does_not_leak` (scope-restriction pinned), `loop_body_move_produces_maybe_partial` (while-loop conservatism), `e0371_does_not_fire_on_copy_binding_after_asymmetric_branch` (Copy fast path), `diverging_match_arms_excluded` (all-arms-diverge fallback). Updated: `for_range_loop_var_scoped_to_body` reflects the new correct scoping. **Test total: 446** (366 library + 69 e2e + 11 LSP), 0 warnings, 0 ignored. All 24 sample programs still compile clean.
  - **What's deferred to 5BC.3+**: method-call move detection (`x.consume()` where `consume` takes `move self`); return-borrow tracking with single-param elision Rule E1 (E0372); self-method elision Rule E2; multi-param elision Rule E3 (`longest` accepts, E0373); partial-place tracking (E0374); replacing sema's linear E0335 with borrowck's flow-sensitive form so E0371 starts firing in user-visible cases.
- **Phase 5 slice 5BC.2a (Copy oracle + E0370 + pipeline wiring) landed:** borrowck is now in the `cpc build` / `cpc check` / `cpc-lsp` pipelines and emits its first real diagnostic. Three additions to [cplus-core/src/borrowck.rs](cplus-core/src/borrowck.rs):
  - **`CopyOracle`** — mirrors sema's struct + enum Copy fixpoint, computed from the AST so borrowck can answer "is this type Copy?" without sema integration. Drop structs are non-Copy unconditionally (matches §3F); aggregates use structural propagation. `definitely_non_copy()` gates diagnostics — returns true only when we *know* the type is non-Copy (unknown / primitive / Copy = false), so unknown-typed bindings never false-fire.
  - **Per-binding type tracking** — parameter types (always explicit), annotated lets (`let x: T = ...`), method receiver (`self` synthesized as the impl block's target), and for-range loop var (synthesized i32). Unannotated lets stay `BindingType::Unknown` and skip Copy gating. **Owned → Moved transitions are now Copy-gated**: `move x: i32` (Copy) keeps the source binding Owned; only non-Copy bindings transition.
  - **E0370 — move-and-shared-borrow of the same place in one call**: scans every move-position arg's binding for reads in sibling argument expressions; emits when the binding is provably non-Copy. Catches the case sema's linear E0335 misses (read-arg evaluated *before* move-arg). Each E0370 carries a `MaybeIncorrect` suggestion describing the two-statement rewrite.
  - **Wired into pipeline** at both invocation sites in [cpc/src/main.rs](cpc/src/main.rs) (project mode `cpc build` and single-file mode) and both sites in [cpc-lsp/src/main.rs](cpc-lsp/src/main.rs) (manifest project mode + open-file single-file mode). Hard-fails on `Severity::Error`; renders alongside sema diagnostics through the same `Diagnostic` pipeline.
  - **Tests**: 10 new unit tests (5 CopyOracle: drop-struct non-Copy, plain-struct Copy, unknown-type-not-definitely-non-Copy, non-Copy propagation through fields, primitives-are-Copy; 2 Copy-gated transitions: i32 move stays Owned, B move transitions to Moved; 5 E0370 cases: positive fire, Copy no-fire, no-sibling-read no-fire, unknown-type no-fire, suggestion attached) + 1 new e2e (`move_and_borrow_in_same_call_rejected` — read-arg-first ordering that sema's E0335 doesn't catch). Test total: **439** (359 library + 69 e2e + 11 LSP), 0 warnings, 0 ignored. All 24 sample programs still compile clean.
  - **What's deferred to 5BC.2b**: branch-merging snapshots at `if` / `match` / loops (produces the `MaybePartial` state), E0371 (use of possibly-moved binding across branches), method-call move detection (`x.consume()` where `consume` takes `move self`). 5BC.3+ adds return-borrow tracking + lifetime elision (E0372, E0373); 5BC.5 adds partial-place tracking (E0374).
- **Phase 5 slice 5BC.1 (borrow-checker place-state machinery) landed:** new module [cplus-core/src/borrowck.rs](cplus-core/src/borrowck.rs) with `Place { root, projections }` (projections empty in 5BC.1 — partial-place tracking lands in 5BC.5), `PlaceState { Owned | BorrowedShared(N) | Moved | MaybePartial }` (only Owned/Moved transitions produced; the other two variants are forward-compatible plumbing for 5BC.2/5BC.3), and a `analyze(prog) -> ProgramAnalysis` entry point that walks every `Function` and `impl` method body, recording `entry` / `after stmt N` / `exit` snapshots. Methods are keyed `Type.method` to match codegen dot-mangling. **One real state transition is produced**: a plain `Ident(name)(args)` call where the callee's signature has a `move`-marked parameter transitions the matching argument-position binding Owned → Moved (covers the `consume(move x)` pattern). Method-call moves, path-call moves, `move self` calls, and branch merging at if/match/loop joins are all 5BC.2 work. **Shadow mode** — module is exposed via `cplus-core/src/lib.rs` but NOT wired into the `cpc build` / `cpc check` / LSP pipelines; no diagnostics are emitted; tests inspect output via `ProgramAnalysis::dump()` (stable canonical text for snapshot assertions). 14 new unit tests covering Place canonicalization, PlaceState::merge for every state pair, entry/exit shape, parameter recording, let-binding entry, move-event transition, non-move call preserves Owned, method analysis key shape, both-branch-walk on `if`, for-range loop-var introduction, and deterministic output. Test total: **428** (349 library + 68 e2e + 11 LSP), 0 warnings, 0 ignored. Wiring into the pipeline + first borrow-checker diagnostic (E0370 move-and-borrow in one call) lands in 5BC.2.
- **Phase 5 borrow-shared design note landed:** [docs/design/phase5-borrow-shared.md](docs/design/phase5-borrow-shared.md). The load-bearing Phase-5 design — Phase-3 move tracking extended to a flow-sensitive, place-granularity borrow checker. Tracks shared borrows of `x: T` / `self` on non-`Copy` types; rejects (a) move-and-borrow of the same place in one call (E0354 → renumber to E0370), (b) use of possibly-moved binding across branches (E0355 / E0371), (c) move while a return-value borrow is live (E0356 / E0372), (d) return of a borrow from a moved-in parameter (E0357 / E0373), (e) partial-place conflicts (E0358 / E0374). Three elision rules: E1 single-parameter, E2 self-method, E3 multi-parameter (body-flow analysis decides which params the return borrows from — the `longest` case). Bias: elide less rather than more (one-way door). Phase 5 introduces lifetimes *conceptually* via diagnostics; Phase 6 introduces them syntactically. Diagnostic surface treated as the long pole — every borrow error carries primary span (the failure), secondary span (the conflict cause), and a fix suggestion. Slicing: 5BC.1 place-state machinery → 5BC.2 within-body conflicts → 5BC.3 single-param elision → 5BC.4 multi-param elision (`longest` accepts here) → 5BC.5 partial-place tracking → 5BC.6 diagnostic polish. **Error-code numbering correction:** §6.1 of the note flagged that E0354–E0360 are owned by [phase5-attributes.md](docs/design/phase5-attributes.md); borrow-checker codes start at **E0370** instead. The note's text uses both — implementation reads the §6.1 table.
- **Phase 5 doctests design note landed:** [docs/design/phase5-doctests.md](docs/design/phase5-doctests.md). `///` triple-slash starts doc comments; triple-backtick fences inside extract as synthesized `#[test] fn DOC_TEST::<qualified_name>` functions in the same file as the documented item. Same-file access rules apply (private helpers callable from doctests); cross-file imports must appear inside the fence (no inheritance of parent file's imports — verbosity exposes the rule per §2.8c). Extraction is a pre-parser pass — preserves span attribution so doctest diagnostics point at the user's doc-comment line, not the synthesized wrapper. `DOC_TEST::` name prefix reserved (E0361); empty fence treatment open (E0362 reserved). Untagged fences only in Phase 5 (no `ignore` / `no_run` / `compile_fail` yet). Doesn't violate §2.8 / §2.8d — extractor is a compiler tool, not user-writable; fenced content is ordinary C+ compiled through the regular pipeline. Implementation blocked on `cpc test` (which is blocked on the borrow checker per the Phase 5 sequencing block in §3).
- **Phase 5 attributes design note landed:** [docs/design/phase5-attributes.md](docs/design/phase5-attributes.md). Defines `#[NAME]` and `#[NAME(args)]` syntax attaching to items only (fn / struct / enum / method / field / variant); attributes are pure data on AST nodes that compiler stages or external tools read — never AST transformation. Phase 5 ships exactly `#[test]`; unknown attributes rejected with did-you-mean (E0354). First instantiation `#[test]` accepts `fn()` / `fn() -> i32`, rejects `pub`, rejects placement inside `impl`; discovery walks the merged Program after sema; `cpc test` synthesizes a driver `main` that calls each test in turn, emits per-test JSON via `--json`; `assert EXPR;` lowers to test-context failure flag (non-test contexts trap). Reserves E0354–E0360. Resolves the §11 `#[test]` vs `test fn` carry-forward in favor of `#[test]`. Implementation blocked on borrow checker per the Phase 5 sequencing block in §3.
- **Phase 4 slice 4-end (break/continue/loop/while-let + cross-file variant patterns + 5-file sample) landed:** closes the small carry-forward items from earlier slices. AST gains `Break`, `Continue`, `Loop(Block)`, `WhileLet`. Parser wires the four constructs (with one-token lookahead distinguishing `while let` from `while`). Lowering rewrites `while let PAT = E { BODY }` → `loop { match E { PAT => BODY, _ => break } }`. Sema's `loop_depth` field gates `break`/`continue` (new **E0353**). Codegen pushes `(continue_label, break_label)` on every loop entry; for-range and C-style for route `continue` through a `step` block so the increment runs first. `stmt_diverges` now recognizes `break`/`continue` (means guard-let else blocks can end in them). Resolver's `rewrite_pattern` now splits `prefix::Enum::Variant` patterns and rewrites the enum prefix via the import alias (closes a 4A carry-forward). 1 new sample [loops.cplus](docs/examples/loops.cplus); new 5-file project [docs/examples/projects/calc/](docs/examples/projects/calc/) covers the Phase-4 modules story end-to-end and satisfies the "project split across 5+ files" exit criterion. Test total: **414** (335 library + 68 e2e + 11 LSP), 0 warnings.
- **Phase 4 slice 4E.3 (LSP goto-definition) landed:** `textDocument/definition` handler re-lexes the buffer at the cursor's byte position to find the identifier, then scans the resolver's merged program (project mode) or the parsed buffer (single-file mode) for items whose qualified name's last `.`-segment matches. Returns a `Location` pointing at the item's name span; uses each origin file's `LineMap`. Works for `fn`, `struct`, `enum` items. Method goto-def (clicking `p.translate()` → `fn translate`) deferred to Phase 5+ when sema's symbol table can answer position-to-symbol queries. 3 new e2e tests (`definition_single_file_jumps_to_fn_declaration`, `definition_project_mode_jumps_across_files`, `definition_on_keyword_returns_empty`). Capability advertised as `true`. Closes the LSP triad: diagnostics + formatting + jump.
- **VS Code editor integration landed (alongside slice 4E.2):** minimal extension under [editors/vscode/](editors/vscode/). `package.json` declares the `cplus` language for `.cplus`, registers a TextMate grammar (`syntaxes/cplus.tmLanguage.json`) covering comments / strings / numbers (incl. type-suffixed and hex/oct/bin) / keyword categories (control, declaration, modifier, other) / built-in + PascalCase types / function definitions and call sites / operator categories / attributes / `import "..." as N` alias coloring, and ships a brackets-and-comments `language-configuration.json`. `extension.js` (~50 lines plain JS, no TypeScript build) spawns `cpc lsp` via `vscode-languageclient` and forwards diagnostics + formatting + code-action requests. Two settings: `cplus.cpcPath` (default `cpc`), `cplus.trace.server`. `.vscode/launch.json` provides the F5 Extension Development Host launch task. Install paths: F5 dev mode or `vsce package` → "Install from VSIX". Tested: `npm install` succeeds, JS / JSON parse clean.
- **Phase 4 slice 4E.2 (LSP formatting + code-action quick-fixes) landed:** `textDocument/formatting` wraps `cplus-core/fmt::format_source` (single whole-document `TextEdit` or empty on canonical input). `textDocument/codeAction` lifts each diagnostic's `(span, replacement)` suggestions into editor Quick Fixes; `is_preferred = true` for `MachineApplicable`. New `ServerState.last_diagnostics` cache holds the raw cplus-core diagnostics (the LSP shape strips suggestion data) so the code-action handler can reach them. Manifest probing now surfaces E0406 / E0407 through the diagnostic pipeline instead of silently falling back to single-file mode (caught by the 4E.2 e2e test on a bad-edition `Cplus.toml`). Tests: 4 new e2e (`formatting_returns_text_edit`, `formatting_returns_no_edits_for_canonical_source`, `code_action_offers_quickfix_for_manifest_edition_error`, `code_action_empty_when_no_diagnostics_overlap`). Test total: **406** (334 library + 64 e2e + 8 LSP), 0 warnings.
- **Phase 4 slice 4E.1 (`cpc-lsp` skeleton + live diagnostics) landed:** new `cpc-lsp/` binary alongside `cpc/`, both linking `cplus-core` (the third tool in the compiler-as-library family). Stdio JSON-RPC via `lsp-server` + `lsp-types` (rust-analyzer family, sync, no tokio). `cpc lsp` subcommand on the `cpc` binary discovers `cpc-lsp` next to itself or on PATH and spawns it. Pushes diagnostics on `didOpen` / `didSave`; per-keystroke `didChange` updates buffer state but does NOT recompute (save-triggered fits the AI-iteration loop; per-keystroke deferred until incremental parsing). Project mode via `Cplus.toml` walk-up from the open file's directory (re-detected on every check); single-file mode otherwise. Every C+ `Diagnostic` mapped mechanically to LSP `Diagnostic` (severity, code-as-string, 1-based → 0-based positions, `source = "cpc"`); cross-file errors push to each originating file's URI. Connection-lifetime fix: main loop takes `Connection` by value so its sender drops on return, unblocking io-thread join (caught the first try-to-shutdown hang in integration tests). 4 e2e tests drive the spawned binary with framed JSON-RPC and assert response shapes. Formatting + goto-def + pull-diagnostics deferred to 4E.2 / 4E.3. Design note: [docs/design/phase4-lsp.md](docs/design/phase4-lsp.md). Test total: **402** (334 library + 64 e2e + 4 LSP), 0 warnings.
- **Phase 4 slice 4D (`cpc fmt`, preserving formatter) landed:** new `cplus-core/src/fmt.rs` module + `cpc fmt` subcommand with `--check` / `--emit` / `--stdin`. Approach: tokenize with trivia (lexer's new `tokenize_with_trivia` emits `LineComment` / `BlockComment` tokens), then walk the token stream; same-line spacing comes from a small (prev, curr) lookup; newlines come from counting newlines in source byte gaps; indent comes from a multi-line-bracket stack; continuation lines preserve user's literal whitespace. Every sample in `docs/examples/` round-trips identical — that's the load-bearing test. Design note: [docs/design/phase4-fmt.md](docs/design/phase4-fmt.md). Reformatting heuristics (collapse incidental wraps, force multi-line on overflow) deferred to 4D.2. Two typo cleanups in `nested.cplus` (incidental double-spaces) landed alongside. Test total: **398** (334 library + 64 e2e), 0 warnings.
- **Phase 4 slice 4C (E0401–E0410 structured diagnostics + did-you-mean) landed:** resolver and manifest errors now flow through `Diagnostic` instead of `eprintln!`. `load_project` returns `LoadFailure { error, sources: BTreeMap<PathBuf, String> }` on failure so the driver has the per-file source to render `--diagnostics=human` snippets against the right file. `LoadFailure::to_diagnostic` builds the structured form with proper line/col + suggestions; `ManifestError::to_diagnostic` does the same for manifest errors (E0406 / E0407). E0401 carries a `MaybeIncorrect` did-you-mean suggestion: scan the importing file's directory tree (up to one level down) for `.cplus` files and propose the closest basename by Levenshtein distance (cutoff 2). 3 new e2e tests pin the JSON shape (E0401 with `primary.file` ending in `main.cplus`), the did-you-mean replacement text, and E0406 routing. Closes the open polish item from the prior 4C entry. Test total: **383** (325 library + 58 e2e), 0 warnings.
- **Phase 4 slice 4C (per-file source threading) landed:** sema's new `check_multi` entry threads the resolver's `BTreeMap<FileId, (PathBuf, String)>` map through to diagnostics. `SemaCx` carries a `BTreeMap<FileId, FileCtx>` (path + source + LineMap); `err()` consults `current_file` (set per-item by every top-level item-iteration pass) to pick the right context. Cross-file errors — including the E0302 inside an imported `math.cplus` from the new test — render with the originating file's path + line/col, not the entry file's. Single-file `check()` now wraps `check_multi` with an empty file map. New e2e test `cross_file_sema_error_renders_in_imported_file` pins the behavior. Test total: **380** (325 library + 55 e2e), 0 warnings. Closes the last slice-4B carry-forward item; E0401–E0410 suggestion-text polish still open and carried to slice 4D.
- **Phase 4 slice 4C (partial — parser polish + field-pub enforcement) landed:** two of the three slice-4B carry-forward items closed in the first 4C session. Parser accepts cross-file struct literals `prefix::Type { ... }` (path-segment loop now defers to a `parse_struct_lit_body` helper when followed by `{` and `no_struct_lit` is off). Sema enforces `pub` on struct fields: `StructDef.fields` is now `Vec<(name, Ty, is_pub)>`, `Item` gained `origin_file: Option<String>` (populated by resolver during merge), and sema tracks `current_file` per item; `check_field` and `check_struct_lit` fire E0403 with "field … is private" when access crosses a file boundary. Resolver's E0403/Struct test switched from the type-position workaround to the natural construction form. 4 new e2e tests + 2 new parser tests.
- **Phase 4 slice 4B (`pub` visibility) landed:** `pub` keyword now parsed and enforced on `fn`, `struct`, `enum`, methods inside `impl`, and individual struct fields. Default private. Same-file references ignore `pub`; cross-file references gated by E0403. Resolver tracks per-file pub_items / pub_methods / item_kind; `check_pub_item` + `check_pub_method` fire at each cross-file qualification site. `pub impl` rejected — methods carry their own pub. Enum variants inherit the enum's pub (no per-variant flag, per design). E0403 variants: Function / Struct / Enum / Method. Field-pub parsed but not yet enforced (deferred to 4C alongside per-file source threading and parser polish for cross-file struct literals). hello_mods updated to use `pub fn square` and a private `double` helper. Test total: **373** (323 library + 50 e2e), 0 warnings.
- **Phase 4 slice 4A.5 (`if let` / `guard let` pattern-binding sugar) landed:** new `guard` keyword + `if let` / `guard let` statement forms; lowering pass [cplus-core/src/lower.rs](cplus-core/src/lower.rs) rewrites them to match-using AST before sema, emitting E0347 (irrefutable `if let`), E0348 (non-diverging guard-let else), E0350 (complement overlap), E0351 (guard-let pattern binds nothing), E0352 (multi-binding deferred). Single-binding only in 4A.5; `while let` deferred (blocked on `break`/`continue` as statements). Sema's match-arm type unification taught to skip syntactically-diverging arms so the guard-let desugar type-checks. Reframed §2.4 (pattern-match sugar is in a different category from `try`/`!T` — no FFI implication) and §2.8c ("verbosity exposes hidden rules; sugar exposes structure" — both apply). Motivation: nested `match` chains hid the success path; pattern-binding sugar exposes structure. Design note: [docs/design/phase4-pattern-let.md](docs/design/phase4-pattern-let.md). Test total: **359** (311 library + 48 e2e), 0 warnings.
- **Phase 4 slice 4A (manifest + multi-file driver) landed:** `import "path.cplus" as name;` syntax (lexer + parser + AST); `Cplus.toml` minimum schema with `toml` crate; multi-file resolver that walks the import graph, dedups via canonical paths, detects cycles (E0404), and rewrites cross-file paths to file-id-qualified names (`src.math.square`) so sema and codegen are unchanged. Entry binary's `fn main()` stays un-prefixed for the linker. New `cpc build` subcommand + `--emit-ll-project`. Sample [hello_mods](docs/examples/projects/hello_mods/) project builds and runs (`49`). Active error codes: E0401 import-not-found, E0404 cycle, E0405 duplicate prefix, E0407 missing manifest entry. Limitations carried to 4B/4C: no `pub` enforcement, no per-file source threading for cross-file diagnostics, no cross-file variant patterns, single `[[bin]]` only. Test total: **344** (301 library + 43 e2e), 0 warnings.
- **Phase 4 modules redesigned (post-discussion, 2026-05-11):** filesystem-driven namespace rule dropped; replaced with mandatory-prefix path-string imports (`import "math.cplus" as math;`). `::` retained for namespace access (§2.8a). No narrowing imports; one mechanism. Rationale: simultaneously closes the root-module-naming, file-vs-dir-collision, and aliasing open questions by structural simplification rather than by picking answers. `mod` keyword reservation dropped. Sample project layout reframed (directories are organizational only). See [docs/design/phase4-modules.md](docs/design/phase4-modules.md). The four old open questions (module aliasing, naming the root module, file/dir collision, enum-variant `pub`) are resolved-by-redesign except the enum-variant question, which stays answered separately as all-or-nothing.
- AI-native: tooling moved out of Phase 11 into Phases 1, 4, 5
- Speculative kept on roadmap: (17) effect tracking, (18) contracts (Phase 7+ design exploration)
- Speculative dropped: (19) capability-based imports
